text-body md:px-4 md:pb-20 relative" role="main"><article><div class="flex flex-col sm:flex-row sm:items-center justify-between gap-4 mb-6"><h1 id="pipe-api" class="t-h3" data-pagefind-weight="20.0">Pipe API<a class="headerlink" href="#pipe-api" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h1><div class="flex-shrink-0 w-auto"><div class="relative inline-block w-auto" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><div class="flex rounded-md overflow-hidden border border-v-border-02 hover:border-v-border-03 transition-colors"><button class="flex items-center gap-1.5 px-3 py-1.5 text-sm transition-colors min-w-[106px] text-v-text-01"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="w-4 h-4 dark:invert-[0.85] dark:brightness-[0.9]"><path d="M14 2H6a2 2 0 0 0-2 2v16a2 2 0 0 0 2 2h12a2 2 0 0 dark:brightness-[0.9]" style="margin-top:-4px;margin-left:-4px"><path fill="currentColor" d="M8.1 11.41 4 6.995 4.745 6 8.1 9.795 11.454 6l.746.994z"></path></svg></button></div></div></div></div><article><div class="my-4 flex items-start gap-2 py-3 px-4 rounded border border-v-border bg-v-callout-info text-code"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="inline shrink-0 mt-px h-5"><path fill="currentColor" d="M7.86 9.742a1 1 0 0 0-.08.1.5.5 0 0 0-.06.12.4.4 0 0 0-.04.12 1 1 0 0 0 0 .134.56.56 0 0 0 .053.253.6.6 0 0 0 .36.36.63.63 0 0 0 .507 0 .6.6 0 0 0 .36-.36.7.7 0 0 0 .04-.253.667.667 0 0 0-1.14-.474m.473-8.86a6.667 6.667 0 1 0 0 13.334 6.667 6.667 0 0 0 0-13.334m0 12a5.333 5.333 0 1 1 0-10.666 5.333 5.333 0 0 1 0 10.666m0-8.666a2 2 0 0 0-1.733 1 .667.667 0 1 0 1.153.666.667.667 0 0 1 1.052-.138.667.667 0 0 1-.472 1.138.667.667 0 0 0-.666.667v.667a.667.667 0 0 0 1.333 0v-.12a2 2 0 0 0-.667-3.88"></path></svg><div class="text-v-text"><p>The API host in the following examples must match your Workspace&#x27;s region. See the full list of <a href="/docs/api-reference#regions-and-endpoints">regions and hosts</a></p></div></div></article><article><p>The Pipes API helps you interact with your Pipes. Several services are included under Pipes:</p><ul><li><a href="#pipes">Pipes</a>: List, create, update, or delete your Tinybird Pipes.</li><li><a href="/docs/api-reference/pipe-api/api-endpoints">API Endpoints</a>: Publish or unpublish your Pipes as API Endpoints.</li><li><a href="/docs/api-reference/pipe-api/materialized-views">Materialized Views and Populates</a>: Create, delete, or populate Materialized Views.</li><li><a href="/docs/api-reference/pipe-api/copy-pipes-api">Scheduled Copy (Copy Pipes API)</a>: Create, delete, schedule, and trigger Copy jobs.</li></ul></article><p>All Tinybird API Endpoints require authentication <a href="/docs/forward/administration/tokens">using a Token</a> with the appropriate scope.</p><div class="my-4 flex items-start gap-2 py-3 px-4 rounded border border-v-border bg-v-callout-caution text-[#856100]"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="inline shrink-0 mt-px h-5"><path fill="currentColor" d="M8.333 10.216a.666.666 0 1 0 0 1.332.666.666 0 0 0 0-1.332m7.114.98L10.08 1.862a2 2 0 0 0-3.493 0l-5.334 9.334a2 2 0 0 0 1.707 3.02h10.747a2 2 0 0 0 1.74-3.02m-1.154 1.333a.67.67 0 0 1-.586.34H2.96a.67.67 0 0 1-.587-.34.67.67 0 0 1 0-.667L7.707 2.53a.667.667 0 0 1 1.186 0l5.367 9.333a.67.67 0 0 1 .033.68zm-5.96-7.647a.667.667 0 0 0-.666.667v2.667a.667.667 0 1 0 1.333 0V5.549a.667.667 0 0 0-.667-.667"></path></svg><div class="text-v-text"><p>Adding or modifying pipes or data sources in <a href="/docs/forward/install-tinybird/local">Tinybird Local</a> and <a href="/docs/forward">Tinybird Forward</a> can only be done through deployments.</p></div></div><h2 id="example-create-a-tinybird-pipe" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Example: create a Tinybird Pipe<a class="headerlink" href="#example-create-a-tinybird-pipe" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Imagine you have an events Data Source named <code>app_events</code> and you want to expose an API Endpoint containing the aggregation of events per day.</p><p>First, create a Pipe called <code>events_per_day</code>:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="creating a Pipe from a Data Source">creating a Pipe from a Data Source</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">curl \
-H &quot;Authorization: Bearer &lt;token&gt;&quot; \
-d &quot;name=events_per_day&amp;sql=select * from app_events&quot; \
https://&lt;your_host&gt;/v0/pipes
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>In the previous snippet, creating the Pipe also defines the first transformation node SQL query, which in this case gets all the data from the Data Source.</p><p>The following JSON example shows a successful request response after creating a Pipe:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="Pipe successfully created">Pipe successfully created</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">{
  &quot;id&quot;: &quot;t_1b501ccf34764a69aaf886bac9a7a6d8&quot;,
  &quot;name&quot;: &quot;events_per_day&quot;,
  &quot;published_version&quot;: &quot;t_878a81f0e1344a2ca990c8c1aa7dd69f&quot;,
  &quot;published_date&quot;: &quot;2019-06-14 09:46:07.884855&quot;,
  &quot;nodes&quot;: [
    {
      &quot;name&quot;: &quot;events_per_day_0&quot;,
      &quot;sql&quot;: &quot;select * from app_events&quot;,
      &quot;id&quot;: &quot;t_878a81f0e1344a2ca990c8c1aa7dd69f&quot;,
      &quot;dependencies&quot;: [
        &quot;app_events&quot;
      ],
      &quot;materialized&quot;: false,
      &quot;created_at&quot;: &quot;2019-06-14 09:46:07.884849&quot;
    }
  ]
}
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Add a new transformation node to perform the aggregation per date, using the previously created node <code>events_per_day_0</code>:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="appending a new node to transform your data">appending a new node to transform your data</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">curl -d &quot;select toDate(timestamp) date, count() event_count from events_per_day_0 group by date&quot; \
  -H &quot;Authorization: Bearer &lt;token&gt;&quot; \
  https://&lt;your_host&gt;/v0/pipes/events_per_day/nodes
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Whenever a transformation node is added to a Pipe, you receive a response like the following, which summarizes the response and provides an autogenerated name for the node, as well as some metadata such as the dependencies with other transformation nodes:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="successful response">successful response</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">{
  &quot;name&quot;: &quot;events_per_day_1&quot;,
  &quot;sql&quot;: &quot;select toDate(timestamp) date, count() event_count from events_per_day_0 group by date&quot;,
  &quot;id&quot;: &quot;t_5164622050b244338ea2b79c19bd1e57&quot;,
  &quot;dependencies&quot;: [
    &quot;events_per_day_0&quot;
  ],
  &quot;materialized&quot;: false,
  &quot;created_at&quot;: &quot;2019-06-14 09:58:08.311812&quot;
}
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>To make a Pipe publicly accessible through the API, activate your desired transformation node as an API Endpoint. Pipes only support one enabled node each, so enabling one makes previously enabled nodes inaccessible.</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="Enabling a transformation node as an API Endpoint">Enabling a transformation node as an API Endpoint</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">curl \
  -X PUT \
  -H &quot;Authorization: Bearer &lt;token&gt;&quot; \
  -d t_878a81f0e1344a2ca990c8c1aa7dd69f \
  https://&lt;your_host&gt;/v0/pipes/events_per_day/endpoint
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>When enabling a transformation node as an API Endpoint, a JSON containing the full Pipe description is sent as the response.</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="Successful response">Successful response</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">{

</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>After creating the Pipe and enabling a transformation node as an Endpoint, you can easily integrate it into any third-party application.</p><p>Using the <a href="/docs/api-reference/query-api">Query API</a>, you can query the Pipe using its name, like a regular table in a SQL query:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="Querying a Pipe using SQL">Querying a Pipe using SQL</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">curl \
-H &quot;Authorization: Bearer &lt;token&gt;&quot; \
-d &#x27;SELECT * FROM events_per_day where date &gt; yesterday()&#x27; \
&#x27;https://&lt;your_host&gt;/v0/sql&#x27;
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><div class="my-4 flex items-start gap-2 py-3 px-4 rounded border border-v-border bg-v-callout-info text-code"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="inline shrink-0 mt-px h-5"><path fill="currentColor" d="M7.86 9.742a1 1 0 0 0-.08.1.5.5 0 0 0-.06.12.4.4 0 0 0-.04.12 1 1 0 0 0 0 .134.56.56 0 0 0 .053.253.6.6 0 0 0 .36.36.63.63 0 0 0 .507 0 .6.6 0 0 0 .36-.36.7.7 0 0 0 .04-.253.667.667 0 0 0-1.14-.474m.473-8.86a6.667 6.667 0 1 0 0 13.334 0-.666.667v.667a.667.667 0 0 0 1.333 0v-.12a2 2 0 0 0-.667-3.88"></path></svg><div class="text-v-text"><p>If you don&#x27;t need to run any special operations against your Pipe, you can use the Pipe data Endpoint accessible at <code>{% user(&quot;apiHost&quot;) %}/v0/pipes/events_per_day.json</code>. It&#x27;s an alias for <code>SELECT * FROM events_per_day</code>.</p></div></div><p>Pipes are updated in real time, so as you insert the new data in <code>app_events</code> Data Source, every Pipe using it <code>events_per_day</code> is updated.</p><p>To share this endpoint, you can create a READ token. You can add a new token for the Pipe with:</p><blockquote><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="Adding a READ Token to an API Endpoint Pipe">Adding a READ Token to an API Endpoint Pipe</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">curl -X POST &quot;https://&lt;your_host&gt;/v0/tokens/?name=events_per_day_token&amp;scope=PIPES:READ:events_per_day&quot;
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div></blockquote><h2 id="pipes" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Pipes<a class="headerlink" href="#pipes" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><div class="max-w-full overflow-x-auto"><div class="body" role="main">
            
  <dl class="http get">
<dt class="sig sig-object http" id="get--v0-pipes-([^-]+)\.(json|csv|ndjson|parquet|prometheus)">
<span class="sig-name descname"><span class="pre">GET</span> </span><span class="sig-name descname"><span class="pre">/v0/pipes/([^/]+)\.(json|csv|ndjson|parquet|prometheus)</span></span><a class="headerlink" href="#get--v0-pipes-([^-]+)\.(json|csv|ndjson|parquet|prometheus)" title="Permalink to this definition">¶</a></dt>
<dd><p>Returns the published node data in a particular format.</p>
<div class="literal-block-wrapper docutils container" id="pipe-get-data">
<div class="code-block-caption"><span class="caption-text">Getting data for a pipe</span><a class="headerlink" href="#pipe-get-data" title="Permalink to this code">¶</a></div>
<div class="highlight-bash notranslate"><div class="highlight"><pre><span></span>curl<span class="w"> </span>-X<span class="w"> </span>GET<span class="w"> </span><span class="se">\</span>
<span class="w">    </span>-H<span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">&quot;Authorization: Bearer &lt;PIPE:READ token&gt;&quot;</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="se">\</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="s2">&quot;<span data-user-custom="apiHost">https://&lt;your_host&gt;</span>/v0/pipes/:name.format&quot;</span>
</pre></div>
</div>
</div>
<table class="docutils align-default" id="pipe-q-parameter">
<caption><span class="caption-text">Request parameters</span><a class="headerlink" href="#pipe-q-parameter" title="Permalink to this table">¶</a></caption>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 20.0%" >
<col style="width: 20.0%" >
<col style="width: 60.0%" >
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr class="row-odd"><th class="head"><p>Key</p></th>
<th class="head"><p>Type</p></th>
<th class="head"><p>Description</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr class="row-even"><td><p>q</p></td>
<td><p>String</p></td>
<td><p>Optional, query to execute, see API Query endpoint</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd"><td><p>output_format_json_quote_64bit_integers</p></td>
<td><p>int</p></td>
<td><p>(Optional) Controls quoting of 64-bit or bigger integers (like UInt64 or Int128) when they are output in a JSON format. Such integers are enclosed in quotes by default. This behavior is compatible with most JavaScript implementations. Possible values: 0 — Integers are output without quotes. 1 — Integers are enclosed in quotes. Default value is 0</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-even"><td><p>output_format_json_quote_denormals</p></td>
<td><p>int</p></td>
<td><p>(Optional) Controls representation of inf and nan on the UI instead of null e.g when dividing by 0 - inf and when there is no representation of a number in Javascript - nan. Possible values: 0 - disabled, 1 - enabled. Default value is 0</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd"><td><p>output_format_parquet_string_as_string</p></td>
<td><p>int</p></td>
<td><p>(Optional) Use Parquet String type instead of Binary for String columns. Possible values: 0 - disabled, 1 - enabled. Default value is 0</p></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<div class="hint docutils container">
<p>The <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">q</span></code> parameter is a SQL query (see <a class="reference external" href="/docs/api-reference/query-api">Query API</a>). When using this endpoint to query your Pipes, you can use the <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">_</span></code> shortcut, which refers to your Pipe name</p>
</div>
<table class="docutils align-default" id="pipe-format-parameter">
<caption><span class="caption-text">Available formats</span><a class="headerlink" href="#pipe-format-parameter" title="Permalink to this table">¶</a></caption>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 20.0%" >
<col style="width: 80.0%" >
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr class="row-odd"><th class="head"><p>format</p></th>
<th class="head"><p>Description</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr class="row-even"><td><p>csv</p></td>
<td><p>CSV with header</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd"><td><p>json</p></td>
<td><p>JSON including data, statistics and schema information</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-even"><td><p>ndjson</p></td>
<td><p>One JSON object per each row</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd"><td><p>parquet</p></td>
<td><p>A Parquet file. Some libraries might not properly process <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">UInt*</span></code> data types, if that’s your case cast those columns to signed integers with <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">toInt*</span></code> functions. <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">String</span></code> columns are exported as <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">Binary</span></code>, take that into account when reading the resulting Parquet file, most libraries convert from Binary to String (e.g. Spark has this configuration param: <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">spark.sql.parquet.binaryAsString</span></code>)</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-even"><td><p>prometheus</p></td>
<td><p>Prometheus text-based format. The output table must include name (String) and value (number) as required columns, with optional help (String), timestamp (number), and type (String) (valid values: counter, gauge, histogram, summary, untyped, or empty). Labels should be a Map(String, String), and rows for the same metric with different labels must appear consecutively. The table must be sorted by the name column.</p></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</dd></dl>

<dl class="http post">
<dt class="sig sig-object http" id="post--v0-pipes-([^-]+)\.(json|csv|ndjson|parquet|prometheus)">
<span class="sig-name descname"><span class="pre">POST</span> </span><span class="sig-name descname"><span class="pre">/v0/pipes/([^/]+)\.(json|csv|ndjson|parquet|prometheus)</span></span><a class="headerlink" href="#post--v0-pipes-([^-]+)\.(json|csv|ndjson|parquet|prometheus)" title="Permalink to this definition">¶</a></dt>
<dd><p>Returns the published node data in a particular format, passing the parameters in the request body. Use this endpoint when the query is too long to be passed as a query string parameter.</p>
<p>When using the post endpoint, there are no traces of the parameters in the pipe_stats_rt Data Source.</p>
<p>See the get endpoint for more information.</p>
</dd></dl>

<dl class="http get">
<dt class="sig sig-object http" id="get--v0-pipes-?">
<span class="sig-name descname"><span class="pre">GET</span> </span><span class="sig-name descname"><span class="pre">/v0/pipes/?</span></span><a class="headerlink" href="#get--v0-pipes-?" title="Permalink to this definition">¶</a></dt>
<dd><p>Get a list of pipes in your account.</p>
<div class="literal-block-wrapper docutils container" id="id1">
<div class="code-block-caption"><span class="caption-text">getting a list of your pipes</span><a class="headerlink" href="#id1" title="Permalink to this code">¶</a></div>
<div class="highlight-bash notranslate"><div class="highlight"><pre><span></span>curl<span class="w"> </span>-X<span class="w"> </span>GET<span class="w"> </span><span class="se">\</span>
<span class="w">    </span>-H<span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">&quot;Authorization: Bearer &lt;PIPE:CREATE token&gt;&quot;</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="se">\</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="s2">&quot;<span data-user-custom="apiHost">https://&lt;your_host&gt;</span>/v0/pipes&quot;</span>
</pre></div>
</div>
</div>
<p>Pipes in the response will be the ones that are accessible using a particular token with read permissions for them.</p>
<div class="literal-block-wrapper docutils container" id="id2">

<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">&quot;ignore_sql_errors&quot;</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">false</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">&quot;node_type&quot;</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">&quot;default&quot;</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="p">}],</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">&quot;url&quot;</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">&quot;<span data-user-custom="apiHost">https://&lt;your_host&gt;</span>/v0/pipes/my_pipe.json&quot;</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="p">}]</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</div>
</div>
<table class="docutils align-default" id="id3">
<caption><span class="caption-text">Request parameters</span><a class="headerlink" href="#id3" title="Permalink to this table">¶</a></caption>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 20.0%" >
<col style="width: 20.0%" >
<col style="width: 60.0%" >
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr class="row-odd"><th class="head"><p>Key</p></th>
<th class="head"><p>Type</p></th>
<th class="head"><p>Description</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr class="row-even"><td><p>dependencies</p></td>
<td><p>boolean</p></td>
<td><p>The response will include the nodes dependent data sources and pipes, default is <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">false</span></code></p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd"><td><p>attrs</p></td>
<td><p>String</p></td>
<td><p>comma separated list of the pipe attributes to return in the response. Example: <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">attrs=name,description</span></code></p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-even"><td><p>node_attrs</p></td>
<td><p>String</p></td>
<td><p>comma separated list of the node attributes to return in the response. Example <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">node_attrs=id,name</span></code></p></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<div class="hint docutils container">
<p>Pipes id’s are immutable so you can always refer to them in your 3rd party applications to make them compatible with Pipes once they are renamed.</p>
</div>
<div class="hint docutils container">
<p>For lighter JSON responses consider using the <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">attrs</span></code> and <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">node_attrs</span></code> params to return exactly the attributes you need to consume.</p>
</div>
</dd></dl>

<dl class="http post">
<dt class="sig sig-object http" id="post--v0-pipes-?">
<span class="sig-name descname"><span class="pre">POST</span> </span><span class="sig-name descname"><span class="pre">/v0/pipes/?</span></span><a class="headerlink" href="#post--v0-pipes-?" title="Permalink to this definition">¶</a></dt>
<dd><p>Creates a new Pipe. There are 3 ways to create a Pipe</p>
<div class="literal-block-wrapper docutils container" id="id4">
<div class="code-block-caption"><span class="caption-text">Creating a Pipe providing full JSON</span><a class="headerlink" href="#id4" title="Permalink to this code">¶</a></div>
<div class="highlight-bash notranslate"><div class="highlight"><pre><span></span>curl<span class="w"> </span>-X<span class="w"> </span>POST<span class="w"> </span><span class="se">\</span>
<span class="w">    </span>-H<span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">&quot;Authorization: Bearer &lt;PIPE:CREATE token&gt;&quot;</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="se">\</span>
<span class="w">    </span>-H<span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">&quot;Content-Type: application/json&quot;</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="se">\</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="s2">&quot;<span data-user-custom="apiHost">https://&lt;your_host&gt;</span>/v0/pipes&quot;</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="se">\</span>
<span class="w">    </span>-d<span class="w"> </span><span class="s1">&#39;{</span>
<span class="s1">        &quot;name&quot;:&quot;pipe_name&quot;,</span>
<span class="s1">        &quot;description&quot;: &quot;my first pipe&quot;,</span>
<span class="s1">        &quot;nodes&quot;: [</span>
<span class="s1">            {&quot;sql&quot;: &quot;select * from my_datasource limit 10&quot;, &quot;name&quot;: &quot;node_00&quot;, &quot;description&quot;: &quot;sampled data&quot; },</span>
<span class="s1">            {&quot;sql&quot;: &quot;select count() from node_00&quot;, &quot;name&quot;: &quot;node_01&quot; }</span>
<span class="s1">        ]</span>
<span class="s1">    }&#39;</span>
</pre></div>
</div>
</div>
<p>If you prefer to create the minimum Pipe, and then append your transformation nodes you can set your name and first transformation node’s SQL in your POST request</p>
<div class="literal-block-wrapper docutils container" id="id5">
<div class="code-block-caption"><span class="caption-text">Creating a pipe with a name and a SQL query</span><a class="headerlink" href="#id5" title="Permalink to this code">¶</a></div>
<div class="highlight-bash notranslate"><div class="highlight"><pre><span></span>curl<span class="w"> </span>-X<span class="w"> </span>POST<span class="w"> </span><span class="se">\</span>
<span class="w">    </span>-H<span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">&quot;Authorization: Bearer &lt;PIPE:CREATE token&gt;&quot;</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="se">\</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="s2">&quot;<span data-user-custom="apiHost">https://&lt;your_host&gt;</span>/v0/pipes?name=pipename&amp;sql=select%20*%20from%20events&quot;</span>
</pre></div>
</div>
</div>
<p>Pipes can be also created as copies of other Pipes. Just use the <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">from</span></code> argument:</p>
<div class="literal-block-wrapper docutils container" id="id6">
<div class="code-block-caption"><span class="caption-text">Creating a pipe from another pipe</span><a class="headerlink" href="#id6" title="Permalink to this code">¶</a></div>
<div class="highlight-bash notranslate"><div class="highlight"><pre><span></span>curl<span class="w"> </span>-X<span class="w"> </span>POST<span class="w"> </span><span class="se">\</span>
<span class="w">    </span>-H<span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">&quot;Authorization: Bearer &lt;PIPE:CREATE token&gt;&quot;</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="se">\</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="s2">&quot;<span data-user-custom="apiHost">https://&lt;your_host&gt;</span>/v0/pipes?name=pipename&amp;from=src_pipe&quot;</span>
</pre></div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="hint docutils container">
<p>Bear in mind, if you use this method to overwrite an existing Pipe, the endpoint will only be maintained if the node name is the same.</p>
</div>
</dd></dl>

<dl class="http post">
<dt class="sig sig-object http" id="post--v0-pipes-(.+)-nodes">
<span class="sig-name descname"><span class="pre">POST</span> </span><span class="sig-name descname"><span class="pre">/v0/pipes/(.+)/nodes</span></span><a class="headerlink" href="#post--v0-pipes-(.+)-nodes" title="Permalink to this definition">¶</a></dt>
<dd><p>Appends a new node to a Pipe.</p>
<div class="literal-block-wrapper docutils container" id="id7">
<div class="code-block-caption"><span class="caption-text">adding a new node to a pipe</span><a class="headerlink" href="#id7" title="Permalink to this code">¶</a></div>
<div class="highlight-bash notranslate"><div class="highlight"><pre><span></span>curl<span class="w"> </span><span class="se">\</span>
<span class="w">    </span>-H<span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">&quot;Authorization: Bearer &lt;PIPE:CREATE token&gt;&quot;</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="se">\</span>
<span class="w">    </span>-d<span class="w"> </span><span class="s1">&#39;select * from node_0&#39;</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">&quot;<span data-user-custom="apiHost">https://&lt;your_host&gt;</span>/v0/pipes/:name/nodes?name=node_name&amp;description=explanation&quot;</span>
</pre></div>
</div>
</div>
<p>Appends a new node that creates a Materialized View</p>
<div class="literal-block-wrapper docutils container" id="id8">
<div class="code-block-caption"><span class="caption-text">adding a Materialized View using a materialized node</span><a class="headerlink" href="#id8" title="Permalink to this code">¶</a></div>
<div class="highlight-bash notranslate"><div class="highlight"><pre><span></span>curl<span class="w"> </span><span class="se">\</span>
<span class="w">    </span>-H<span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">&quot;Authorization: Bearer &lt;PIPE:CREATE token&gt;&quot;</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="se">\</span>
<span class="w">    </span>-d<span class="w"> </span><span class="s1">&#39;select id, sum(amount) as amount, date from my_datasource&#39;</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">&quot;<span data-user-custom="apiHost">https://&lt;your_host&gt;</span>/v0/pipes/:name/nodes?name=node_name&amp;description=explanation&amp;type=materialized&amp;datasource=new_datasource&amp;engine=AggregatingMergeTree&quot;</span>
</pre></div>
</div>
</div>
<table class="docutils align-default" id="id9">
<caption><span class="caption-text">Request parameters</span><a class="headerlink" href="#id9" title="Permalink to this table">¶</a></caption>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 20.0%" >
<col style="width: 20.0%" >
<col style="width: 60.0%" >
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr class="row-odd"><th class="head"><p>Key</p></th>
<th class="head"><p>Type</p></th>
<th class="head"><p>Description</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr class="row-even"><td><p>name</p></td>
<td><p>String</p></td>
<td><p>The referenceable name for the node.</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd"><td><p>description</p></td>
<td><p>String</p></td>
<td><p>Use it to store a more detailed explanation of the node.</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-even"><td><p>token</p></td>
<td><p>String</p></td>
<td><p>Auth token. Ensure it has the <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">PIPE:CREATE</span></code> scope on it</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd"><td><p>type</p></td>
<td><p>String</p></td>
<td><p>Optional. Available options are {<code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">standard</span></code> (default), <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">materialized</span></code>, <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">endpoint</span></code>}. Use <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">materialized</span></code> to create a Materialized View from your new node.</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-even"><td><p>datasource</p></td>
<td><p>String</p></td>
<td><p>Required with <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">type=materialized</span></code>. Specifies the name of the destination Data Source where the Materialized View schema is defined.</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd"><td><p>override_datasource</p></td>
<td><p>Boolean</p></td>
<td><p>Optional. Default <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">false</span></code> When the target Data Source of the Materialized View exists in the Workspace it’ll be overriden by the <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">datasource</span></code> specified in the request.</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-even"><td><p>populate</p></td>
<td><p>Boolean</p></td>
<td><p>Optional. Default <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">false</span></code>. When <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">true</span></code>, a job is triggered to populate the destination Data Source.</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd"><td><p>populate_subset</p></td>
<td><p>Float</p></td>
<td><p>Optional. Populate with a subset percent of the data (limited to a maximum of 2M rows), this is useful to quickly test a materialized node with some data. The subset must be greater than 0 and lower than 0.1. A subset of 0.1 means a 10 percent of the data in the source Data Source will be used to populate the Materialized View. Use it together with <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">populate=true</span></code>, it has precedence over <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">populate_condition</span></code></p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-even"><td><p>populate_condition</p></td>
<td><p>String</p></td>
<td><p>Optional. Populate with a SQL condition to be applied to the trigger Data Source of the Materialized View. For instance, <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">populate_condition='date</span> <span class="pre">==</span> <span class="pre">toYYYYMM(now())'</span></code> it’ll populate taking all the rows from the trigger Data Source which <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">date</span></code> is the current month. Use it together with <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">populate=true</span></code>. <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">populate_condition</span></code> is not taken into account if the <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">populate_subset</span></code> param is present. Including in the <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">populate_condition</span></code> any column present in the Data Source <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">engine_sorting_key</span></code> will make the populate job process less data.</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd"><td><p>unlink_on_populate_error</p></td>
<td><p>String</p></td>
<td><p>Optional. Default is <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">false</span></code>. If the populate job fails the Materialized View is unlinked and new data won’t be ingested in the Materialized View.</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-even"><td><p>engine</p></td>
<td><p>String</p></td>
<td><p>Optional. Engine for destination Materialized View. Requires the <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">type</span></code> parameter as <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">materialized</span></code>.</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd"><td><p>engine_*</p></td>
<td><p>String</p></td>
<td><p>Optional. Engine parameters and options. Requires the <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">type</span></code> parameter as <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">materialized</span></code> and the <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">engine</span></code> parameter. <a class="reference external" href="/docs/api-reference/datasource-api">Check Engine Parameters and Options for more details</a></p></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>SQL query for the transformation node must be sent in the body encoded in utf-8</p>
<table class="docutils align-default" id="id10">
<caption><span class="caption-text">Response codes</span><a class="headerlink" href="#id10" title="Permalink to this table">¶</a></caption>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 20.0%" >
<col style="width: 80.0%" >
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr class="row-odd"><th class="head"><p>Code</p></th>
<th class="head"><p>Description</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr class="row-even"><td><p>200</p></td>
<td><p>No error</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd"><td><p>400</p></td>
<td><p>empty or wrong SQL or API param value</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-even"><td><p>403</p></td>
<td><p>Forbidden. Provided token doesn’t have permissions to append a node to the pipe, it needs <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">ADMIN</span></code> or <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">PIPE:CREATE</span></code></p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd"><td><p>404</p></td>
<td><p>Pipe not found</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-even"><td><p>409</p></td>
<td><p>There’s another resource with the same name, names must be unique | The Materialized View already exists | <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">override_datasource</span></code> cannot be performed</p></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</dd></dl>

<dl class="http delete">
<dt class="sig sig-object http" id="delete--v0-pipes-(.+)-nodes-(.+)">
<span class="sig-name descname"><span class="pre">DELETE</span> </span><span class="sig-name descname"><span class="pre">/v0/pipes/(.+)/nodes/(.+)</span></span><a class="headerlink" href="#delete--v0-pipes-(.+)-nodes-(.+)" title="Permalink to this definition">¶</a></dt>
<dd><p>Drops a particular transformation node in the Pipe. It does not remove related nodes so this could leave the Pipe in an unconsistent state. For security reasons, enabled nodes can’t be removed.</p>
<div class="literal-block-wrapper docutils container" id="id11">
<div class="code-block-caption"><span class="caption-text">removing a node from a pipe</span><a class="headerlink" href="#id11" title="Permalink to this code">¶</a></div>
<div class="highlight-bash notranslate"><div class="highlight"><pre><span></span>curl<span class="w"> </span>-X<span class="w"> </span>DELETE<span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">&quot;<span data-user-custom="apiHost">https://&lt;your_host&gt;</span>/v0/pipes/:name/nodes/:node_id&quot;</span>
</pre></div>
</div>
</div>
<table class="docutils align-default" id="id12">
<caption><span class="caption-text">Response codes</span><a class="headerlink" href="#id12" title="Permalink to this table">¶</a></caption>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 20.0%" >
<col style="width: 80.0%" >
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr class="row-odd"><th class="head"><p>Code</p></th>
<th class="head"><p>Description</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr class="row-even"><td><p>204</p></td>
<td><p>No error, removed node</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd"><td><p>400</p></td>
<td><p>The node is published. Published nodes can’t be removed</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-even"><td><p>403</p></td>
<td><p>Forbidden. Provided token doesn’t have permissions to change the last node of the pipe, it needs ADMIN or IMPORT</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd"><td><p>404</p></td>
<td><p>Pipe not found</p></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</dd></dl>

<dl class="http get">
<dt class="sig sig-object http" id="get--v0-pipes-(.+\.pipe)">
<span class="sig-name descname"><span class="pre">GET</span> </span><span class="sig-name descname"><span class="pre">/v0/pipes/(.+\.pipe)</span></span><a class="headerlink" href="#get--v0-pipes-(.+\.pipe)" title="Permalink to this definition">¶</a></dt>
<dd><p>Get pipe information. Provided Auth Token must have read access to the Pipe.</p>
<div class="literal-block-wrapper docutils container" id="id16">
<div class="code-block-caption"><span class="caption-text">Getting information about a particular pipe</span><a class="headerlink" href="#id16" title="Permalink to this code">¶</a></div>
<div class="highlight-bash notranslate"><div class="highlight"><pre><span></span>curl<span class="w"> </span>-X<span class="w"> </span>GET<span class="w"> </span><span class="se">\</span>
<span class="w">    </span>-H<span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">&quot;Authorization: Bearer &lt;PIPE:READ token&gt;&quot;</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="se">\</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="s2">&quot;<span data-user-custom="apiHost">https://&lt;your_host&gt;</span>/v0/pipes/:name&quot;</span>
</pre></div>
</div>
</div>
<p><code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">pipe_id</span></code> and <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">pipe_name</span></code> are two ways to refer to the pipe in SQL queries and API endpoints the only difference is <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">pipe_id</span></code> never changes so it’ll work even if you change the <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">pipe_name</span></code> (which is the name used to display the pipe). In general you can use <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">pipe_id</span></code> or <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">pipe_name</span></code> indistinctly:</p>
<div class="literal-block-wrapper docutils container" id="id17">
<div class="code-block-caption"><span class="caption-text">Successful response</span><a class="headerlink" href="#id17" title="Permalink to this code">¶</a></div>
<div class="highlight-json notranslate"><div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">&quot;id&quot;</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">&quot;t_bd1c62b5e67142bd9bf9a7f113a2b6ea&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">&quot;name&quot;</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">&quot;events_pipe&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">&quot;pipeline&quot;</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">&quot;nodes&quot;</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">[{</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">&quot;name&quot;</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">&quot;events_ds_0&quot;</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">&quot;sql&quot;</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">&quot;select * from events_ds_log__raw&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">&quot;materialized&quot;</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">false</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="p">},</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">&quot;name&quot;</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">&quot;events_ds&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">&quot;sql&quot;</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">&quot;select * from events_ds_0 where valid = 1&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">&quot;materialized&quot;</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">false</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="p">}]</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="hint docutils container">
<p>You can make your Pipe’s id more descriptive by prepending information such as <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">t_my_events_table.bd1c62b5e67142bd9bf9a7f113a2b6ea</span></code></p>
</div>
</dd></dl>

<dd><p>Drops a Pipe from your account. Auth token in use must have the <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">DROP:NAME</span></code> scope.</p>
<div class="literal-block-wrapper docutils container" id="id18">

            <div class="clearer"></div>
          </div></div><div class="max-w-full overflow-x-auto"><div class="body" role="main">
            
  <dl class="http get">
<dt class="sig sig-object http" id="get--v0-pipes-(.+)-nodes-(.+)-explain">
<span class="sig-name descname"><span class="pre">GET</span> </span><span class="sig-name descname"><span class="pre">/v0/pipes/(.+)/nodes/(.+)/explain</span></span><a class="headerlink" href="#get--v0-pipes-(.+)-nodes-(.+)-explain" title="Permalink to this definition">¶</a></dt>
<dd><p>Return the explain plan and the whole debug query for the node.</p>
<p>If no node is specified, the most relevant node of the pipe will be used:</p>
<ul class="simple">
<li><p>The endpoint node for endpoints.</p></li>
<li><p>The node that materializes for materialized views.</p></li>
<li><p>The copy node for Copy pipes.</p></li>
<li><p>The last node for general pipes.</p></li>
</ul>
<p>It accepts query parameters to test the query with different values.</p>
<div class="literal-block-wrapper docutils container" id="id1">
<div class="code-block-caption"><span class="caption-text">Getting the explain plan</span><a class="headerlink" href="#id1" title="Permalink to this code">¶</a></div>
<div class="highlight-bash notranslate"><div class="highlight"><pre><span></span>curl<span class="w"> </span>-X<span class="w"> </span>GET<span class="w"> </span><span class="se">\</span>
<span class="w">    </span>-H<span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">&quot;Authorization: Bearer &lt;PIPE:READ and DATASOURCE:READ token&gt;&quot;</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="se">\</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="s2">&quot;<span data-user-custom="apiHost">https://&lt;your_host&gt;</span>/v0/pipes/:pipe_name/nodes/:node_name/explain?department=Engineering&quot;</span>

or

curl<span class="w"> </span>-X<span class="w"> </span>GET<span class="w"> </span><span class="se">\</span>
<span class="w">    </span>-H<span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">&quot;Authorization: Bearer &lt;PIPE:READ and DATASOURCE:READ token&gt;&quot;</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="se">\</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="s2">&quot;<span data-user-custom="apiHost">https://&lt;your_host&gt;</span>/v0/pipes/:pipe_name/explain?department=Engineering&quot;</span>
</pre></div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="literal-block-wrapper docutils container" id="id2">
<div class="code-block-caption"><span class="caption-text">Successful response</span><a class="headerlink" href="#id2" title="Permalink to this code">¶</a></div>
<div class="highlight-json notranslate"><div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">&quot;debug_query&quot;</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">&quot;SELECT country, department FROM (SELECT * FROM employees AS employees) AS an_endpoint_0 WHERE department = &#39;Engineering&#39;&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">&quot;query_explain&quot;</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">&quot;Expression ((Projection + Before ORDER BY)) Filter ((WHERE + (Projection + Before ORDER BY))) ReadFromMergeTree (employees) Indexes: MinMax Condition: true Parts: 6/6 Granules: 6/6 Partition Condition: true Parts: 6/6 Granules: 6/6 PrimaryKey Condition: true Parts: 6/6 Granules: 6/6&quot;</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</div>
</div>
<table class="docutils align-default" id="id3">
<caption><span class="caption-text">Request parameters</span><a class="headerlink" href="#id3" title="Permalink to this table">¶</a></caption>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 20.0%" >
<col style="width: 20.0%" >
<col style="width: 60.0%" >
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr class="row-odd"><th class="head"><p>Key</p></th>
<th class="head"><p>Type</p></th>
<th class="head"><p>Description</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr class="row-even"><td><p>token</p></td>
<td><p>String</p></td>
<td><p>Auth token. Ensure it has the <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">PIPE:READ</span></code> and the proper <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">DATASOURCE:READ</span></code> scopes on it.</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd"><td><p>pipe_name</p></td>
<td><p>Float</p></td>
<td><p>The name or id of the pipe.</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-even"><td><p>node_name</p></td>
<td><p>String</p></td>
<td><p>Optional. The name or id of the node to explain. If not provided, the most relevant node of the pipe will be used.</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd"><td><p>params</p></td>
<td><p>String</p></td>
<td><p>Optional. The value of the parameters to test the query with. They are regular URL query parameters.</p></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table class="docutils align-default" id="id4">
<caption><span class="caption-text">Response codes</span><a class="headerlink" href="#id4" title="Permalink to this table">¶</a></caption>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 20.0%" >
<col style="width: 80.0%" >
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr class="row-odd"><th class="head"><p>Code</p></th>
<th class="head"><p>Description</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr class="row-even"><td><p>200</p></td>
<td><p>No error</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd"><td><p>400</p></td>
<td><p>Could not get a node to run the explain plan</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-even"><td><p>403</p></td>
<td><p>Forbidden. Provided token doesn’t have permissions to run the explain plan, it needs <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">ADMIN</span></code> or <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">PIPE:READ</span></code> and <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">DATASOURCE:READ</span></code></p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd"><td><p>404</p></td>
<td><p>Pipe not found, Node not found</p></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</dd></dl>

<dl class="http get">
<dt class="sig sig-object http" id="get--v0-pipes-(.+)-explain">

<dd><p>Return the explain plan and the whole debug query for the node.</p>
<p>If no node is specified, the most relevant node of the pipe will be used:</p>
<ul class="simple">
<li><p>The endpoint node for endpoints.</p></li>

<div class="literal-block-wrapper docutils container" id="id5">

<span class="w">    </span><span class="s2">&quot;<span data-user-custom="apiHost">https://&lt;your_host&gt;</span>/v0/pipes/:pipe_name/explain?department=Engineering&quot;</span>
</pre></div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="literal-block-wrapper docutils container" id="id6">
<div class="code-block-caption"><span class="caption-text">Successful response</span><a class="headerlink" href="#id6" title="Permalink to this code">¶</a></div>
<div class="highlight-json notranslate"><div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">&quot;debug_query&quot;</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">&quot;SELECT country, department FROM (SELECT * FROM employees AS employees) AS an_endpoint_0 WHERE department = &#39;Engineering&#39;&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">&quot;query_explain&quot;</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">&quot;Expression ((Projection + Before ORDER BY)) Filter ((WHERE + (Projection + Before ORDER BY))) ReadFromMergeTree (employees) Indexes: MinMax Condition: true Parts: 6/6 Granules: 6/6 Partition Condition: true Parts: 6/6 Granules: 6/6 PrimaryKey Condition: true Parts: 6/6 Granules: 6/6&quot;</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</div>
</div>

<col style="width: 20.0%" >
<col style="width: 20.0%" >
<col style="width: 60.0%" >
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr class="row-odd"><th class="head"><p>Key</p></th>
<th class="head"><p>Type</p></th>
<th class="head"><p>Description</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr class="row-even"><td><p>token</p></td>
<td><p>String</p></td>
<td><p>Auth token. Ensure it has the <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">PIPE:READ</span></code> and the proper <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">DATASOURCE:READ</span></code> scopes on it.</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd"><td><p>pipe_name</p></td>
<td><p>Float</p></td>
<td><p>The name or id of the pipe.</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-even"><td><p>node_name</p></td>
<td><p>String</p></td>
<td><p>Optional. The name or id of the node to explain. If not provided, the most relevant node of the pipe will be used.</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd"><td><p>params</p></td>
<td><p>String</p></td>
<td><p>Optional. The value of the parameters to test the query with. They are regular URL query parameters.</p></td>
</tr>
</tbody>

<td><p>Forbidden. Pipes API Reference\nmeta:\n    description: The Pipe API enables you to manage your Pipes. With Pipes you can transform data via SQL queries and publish the results of those queries as API Endpoints.\n---\n\n# Pipe API\n\n{% snippet title=\"api-region-reminder\" /%}\n\n{% snippet title=\"pipes-api-snippet\" /%}\n\nAll Tinybird API Endpoints require authentication [using a Token](/forward/administration/tokens) with the appropriate scope.\n\n{% callout type=\"caution\" %}\nAdding or modifying pipes or data sources in [Tinybird Local](/forward/install-tinybird/local) and [Tinybird Forward](/forward) can only be done through deployments.\n{% /callout %}\n\n## Example: create a Tinybird Pipe\n\nImagine you have an events Data Source named `app_events` and you want to expose an API Endpoint containing the aggregation of events per day.\n\nFirst, create a Pipe called `events_per_day`:\n\n```shell {% title=\"creating a Pipe from a Data Source\" %}\ncurl \\\n-H \"Authorization: Bearer \u003ctoken\u003e\" \\\n-d \"name=events_per_day\u0026sql=select * from app_events\" \\\n{% user(\"apiHost\") %}/v0/pipes\n```\n\nIn the previous snippet, creating the Pipe also defines the first transformation node SQL query, which in this case gets all the data from the Data Source. \n\nThe following JSON example shows a successful request response after creating a Pipe:\n\n```json {% title=\"Pipe successfully created\" %}\n{\n  \"id\": \"t_1b501ccf34764a69aaf886bac9a7a6d8\",\n  \"name\": \"events_per_day\",\n  \"published_version\": \"t_878a81f0e1344a2ca990c8c1aa7dd69f\",\n  \"published_date\": \"2019-06-14 09:46:07.884855\",\n  \"nodes\": [\n    {\n      \"name\": \"events_per_day_0\",\n      \"sql\": \"select * from app_events\",\n      \"id\": \"t_878a81f0e1344a2ca990c8c1aa7dd69f\",\n      \"dependencies\": [\n        \"app_events\"\n      ],\n      \"materialized\": false,\n      \"created_at\": \"2019-06-14 09:46:07.884849\"\n    }\n  ]\n}\n```\n\nAdd a new transformation node to perform the aggregation per date, using the previously created node `events_per_day_0`:\n\n```shell {% title=\"appending a new node to transform your data\" %}\ncurl -d \"select toDate(timestamp) date, count() event_count from events_per_day_0 group by date\" \\\n  -H \"Authorization: Bearer \u003ctoken\u003e\" \\\n  {% user(\"apiHost\") %}/v0/pipes/events_per_day/nodes\n```\n\nWhenever a transformation node is added to a Pipe, you receive a response like the following, which summarizes the response and provides an autogenerated name for the node, as well as some metadata such as the dependencies with other transformation nodes:\n\n```json {% title=\"successful response\" %}\n{\n  \"name\": \"events_per_day_1\",\n  \"sql\": \"select toDate(timestamp) date, count() event_count from events_per_day_0 group by date\",\n  \"id\": \"t_5164622050b244338ea2b79c19bd1e57\",\n  \"dependencies\": [\n    \"events_per_day_0\"\n  ],\n  \"materialized\": false,\n  \"created_at\": \"2019-06-14 09:58:08.311812\"\n}\n```\n\nTo make a Pipe publicly accessible through the API, activate your desired transformation node as an API Endpoint. Pipes only support one enabled node each, so enabling one makes previously enabled nodes inaccessible.\n\n```shell {% title=\"Enabling a transformation node as an API Endpoint\" %}\ncurl \\\n  -X PUT \\\n  -H \"Authorization: Bearer \u003ctoken\u003e\" \\\n  -d t_878a81f0e1344a2ca990c8c1aa7dd69f \\\n  {% user(\"apiHost\") %}/v0/pipes/events_per_day/endpoint\n```\n\nWhen enabling a transformation node as an API Endpoint, a JSON containing the full Pipe description is sent as the response.\n\n```json {% title=\"Successful response\" %}\n{\n  \"id\": \"t_1b501ccf34764a69aaf886bac9a7a6d8\",\n  \"name\": \"events_per_day\",\n  \"published_version\": \"t_5164622050b244338ea2b79c19bd1e57\",\n  \"published_date\": \"2019-06-14 10:17:01.201962\",\n  \"nodes\": [\n    {\n      \"name\": \"events_per_day_0\",\n      \"sql\": \"select * from app_events\",\n      \"id\": \"t_878a81f0e1344a2ca990c8c1aa7dd69f\",\n      \"dependencies\": [\n        \"app_events\"\n      ],\n      \"materialized\": false,\n      \"created_at\": \"2019-06-14 10:17:01.201784\"\n    },\n    {\n      \"name\": \"events_per_day_1\",\n      \"sql\": \"select toDate(date) date, count() event_count from events_per_day_0 group by date\",\n      \"id\": \"t_5164622050b244338ea2b79c19bd1e57\",\n      \"dependencies\": [\n        \"events_per_day_0\"\n      ],\n      \"materialized\": false,\n      \"created_at\": \"2019-06-14 10:17:01.201943\"\n    }\n  ]\n}\n```\n\nAfter creating the Pipe and enabling a transformation node as an Endpoint, you can easily integrate it into any third-party application.\n\nUsing the [Query API](/api-reference/query-api), you can query the Pipe using its name, like a regular table in a SQL query:\n\n```shell {% title=\"Querying a Pipe using SQL\" %}\ncurl \\\n-H \"Authorization: Bearer \u003ctoken\u003e\" \\\n-d 'SELECT * FROM events_per_day where date \u003e yesterday()' \\\n'{% user(\"apiHost\") %}/v0/sql'\n```\n\n{% callout %}\nIf you don't need to run any special operations against your Pipe, you can use the Pipe data Endpoint accessible at `{% user(\"apiHost\") %}/v0/pipes/events_per_day.json`. It's an alias for `SELECT * FROM events_per_day`.\n{% /callout %}\n\nPipes are updated in real time, so as you insert the new data in `app_events` Data Source, every Pipe using it `events_per_day` is updated.\n\nTo share this endpoint, you can create a READ token. You can add a new token for the Pipe with:\n\n\u003e ```shell {% title=\"Adding a READ Token to an API Endpoint Pipe\" %}\n\u003e curl -X POST \"{% user(\"apiHost\") %}/v0/tokens/?name=events_per_day_token\u0026scope=PIPES:READ:events_per_day\"\n\u003e ```\n\n## Pipes\n\n{% api_reference api=\"pipe-list\" /%}\n\n{% api_reference api=\"pipe-node-explain\" /%}\n"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"2c:{\"fill\":\"currentColor\",\"d\":\"M7.86 9.742a1 1 0 0 0-.08.1.5.5 0 0 0-.06.12.4.4 0 0 0-.04.12 1 1 0 0 0 0 .134.56.56 0 0 0 .053.253.6.6 0 0 0 .36.36.63.63 0 0 0 .507 0 .6.6 0 0 0 .36-.36.7.7 0 0 0 .04-.253.667.667 0 0 0-1.14-.474m.473-8.86a6.667 6.667 0 1 0 0 13.334 6.667 6.667 0 0 0 0-13.334m0 12a5.333 5.333 0 1 1 0-10.666 5.333 5.333 0 0 1 0 10.666m0-8.666a2 2 0 0 0-1.733 1 .667.667 0 1 0 1.153.666.667.667 0 0 1 1.052-.138.667.667 0 0 1-.472 1.138.667.667 0 0 0-.666.667v.667a.667.667 0 0 0 1.333 0v-.12a2 2 0 0 0-.667-3.88\"}\n2b:[\"$\",\"path\",null,\"$2c\"]\n"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"8:[\"$\",\"div\",null,{\"className\":\"relative max-w-7xl mx-auto px-5 md:px-6 xl:grid Controls quoting of 64-bit or bigger integers (like UInt64 or Int128) when they are output in a JSON format. Such integers are enclosed in quotes by default. This behavior is compatible with most JavaScript implementations. Possible values: 0 — Integers are output without quotes. 1 — Integers are enclosed in quotes. Default value is 0\u003c/p\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr class=\"row-even\"\u003e\u003ctd\u003e\u003cp\u003eoutput_format_json_quote_denormals\u003c/p\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003cp\u003eint\u003c/p\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003cp\u003e(Optional) Controls representation of inf and nan on the UI instead of null e.g when dividing by 0 - inf and when there is no representation of a number in Javascript - nan. When using this endpoint to query your Pipes, you can use the \u003ccode class=\"docutils literal notranslate\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pre\"\u003e_\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e shortcut, which refers to your Pipe name\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003ctable class=\"docutils align-default\" id=\"pipe-format-parameter\"\u003e\n\u003ccaption\u003e\u003cspan class=\"caption-text\"\u003eAvailable formats\u003c/span\u003e\u003ca class=\"headerlink\" href=\"#pipe-format-parameter\" title=\"Permalink to this table\"\u003e¶\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/caption\u003e\n\u003ccolgroup\u003e\n\u003ccol style=\"width: 20.0%\" \u003e\n\u003ccol style=\"width: 80.0%\" \u003e\n\u003c/colgroup\u003e\n\u003cthead\u003e\n\u003ctr class=\"row-odd\"\u003e\u003cth class=\"head\"\u003e\u003cp\u003eformat\u003c/p\u003e\u003c/th\u003e\n\u003cth class=\"head\"\u003e\u003cp\u003eDescription\u003c/p\u003e\u003c/th\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003c/thead\u003e\n\u003ctbody\u003e\n\u003ctr class=\"row-even\"\u003e\u003ctd\u003e\u003cp\u003ecsv\u003c/p\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003cp\u003eCSV with header\u003c/p\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr class=\"row-odd\"\u003e\u003ctd\u003e\u003cp\u003ejson\u003c/p\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003cp\u003eJSON including data, statistics and schema information\u003c/p\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr class=\"row-even\"\u003e\u003ctd\u003e\u003cp\u003endjson\u003c/p\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003cp\u003eOne JSON object per each row\u003c/p\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr class=\"row-odd\"\u003e\u003ctd\u003e\u003cp\u003eparquet\u003c/p\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003cp\u003eA Parquet file. Some libraries might not properly process \u003ccode class=\"docutils literal notranslate\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pre\"\u003eUInt*\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e data types, if that’s your case cast those columns to signed integers with \u003ccode class=\"docutils literal notranslate\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pre\"\u003etoInt*\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e functions. \u003ccode class=\"docutils literal notranslate\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pre\"\u003eString\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e columns are exported as \u003ccode class=\"docutils literal notranslate\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pre\"\u003eBinary\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e, take that into account when reading the resulting Parquet file, most libraries convert from Binary to String (e.g. Spark has this configuration param: \u003ccode class=\"docutils literal notranslate\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pre\"\u003espark.sql.parquet.binaryAsString\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e)\u003c/p\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr class=\"row-even\"\u003e\u003ctd\u003e\u003cp\u003eprometheus\u003c/p\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003cp\u003ePrometheus text-based format. The output table must include name (String) and value (number) as required columns, with optional help (String), timestamp (number), and type (String) (valid values: counter, gauge, histogram, summary, untyped, or empty). Labels should be a Map(String, String), and rows for the same metric with different labels must appear consecutively. The table must be sorted by the name column.\u003c/p\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003c/tbody\u003e\n\u003c/table\u003e\n\u003c/dd\u003e\u003c/dl\u003e\n\n\u003cdl class=\"http post\"\u003e\n\u003cdt class=\"sig sig-object http\" id=\"post--v0-pipes-([^-]+)\\.(json|csv|ndjson|parquet|prometheus)\"\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"sig-name descname\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pre\"\u003ePOST\u003c/span\u003e \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"sig-name descname\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pre\"\u003e/v0/pipes/([^/]+)\\.(json|csv|ndjson|parquet|prometheus)\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003ca class=\"headerlink\" href=\"#post--v0-pipes-([^-]+)\\.(json|csv|ndjson|parquet|prometheus)\" title=\"Permalink to this definition\"\u003e¶\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/dt\u003e\n\u003cdd\u003e\u003cp\u003eReturns the published node data in a particular format, passing the parameters in the request body. Default \u003ccode class=\"docutils literal notranslate\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pre\"\u003efalse\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e When the target Data Source of the Materialized View exists in the Workspace it’ll be overriden by the \u003ccode class=\"docutils literal notranslate\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pre\"\u003edatasource\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e specified in the request.\u003c/p\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr class=\"row-even\"\u003e\u003ctd\u003e\u003cp\u003epopulate\u003c/p\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003cp\u003eBoolean\u003c/p\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003cp\u003eOptional. Default \u003ccode class=\"docutils literal notranslate\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pre\"\u003efalse\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e. When \u003ccode class=\"docutils literal notranslate\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pre\"\u003etrue\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e, a job is triggered to populate the destination Data Source.\u003c/p\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr class=\"row-odd\"\u003e\u003ctd\u003e\u003cp\u003epopulate_subset\u003c/p\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003cp\u003eFloat\u003c/p\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003cp\u003eOptional. Populate with a subset percent of the data (limited to a maximum of 2M rows), this is useful to quickly test a materialized node with some data. The subset must be greater than 0 and lower than 0.1. A subset of 0.1 means a 10 percent of the data in the source Data Source will be used to populate the Materialized View. Use it together with \u003ccode class=\"docutils literal notranslate\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pre\"\u003epopulate=true\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e, it has precedence over \u003ccode class=\"docutils literal notranslate\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pre\"\u003epopulate_condition\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr class=\"row-even\"\u003e\u003ctd\u003e\u003cp\u003epopulate_condition\u003c/p\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003cp\u003eString\u003c/p\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003cp\u003eOptional. Populate with a SQL condition to be applied to the trigger Data Source of the Materialized View. For instance, \u003ccode class=\"docutils literal notranslate\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pre\"\u003epopulate_condition='date\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pre\"\u003e==\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pre\"\u003etoYYYYMM(now())'\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e it’ll populate taking all the rows from the trigger Data Source which \u003ccode class=\"docutils literal notranslate\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pre\"\u003edate\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e is the current month. Use it together with \u003ccode class=\"docutils literal notranslate\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pre\"\u003epopulate=true\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e. \u003ccode class=\"docutils literal notranslate\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pre\"\u003epopulate_condition\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e is not taken into account if the \u003ccode class=\"docutils literal notranslate\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pre\"\u003epopulate_subset\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e param is present. Including in the \u003ccode class=\"docutils literal notranslate\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pre\"\u003epopulate_condition\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e any column present in the Data Source \u003ccode class=\"docutils literal notranslate\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pre\"\u003eengine_sorting_key\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e will make the populate job process less data.\u003c/p\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr class=\"row-odd\"\u003e\u003ctd\u003e\u003cp\u003eunlink_on_populate_error\u003c/p\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003cp\u003eString\u003c/p\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003cp\u003eOptional. Default is \u003ccode class=\"docutils literal notranslate\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pre\"\u003efalse\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e. If the populate job fails the Materialized View is unlinked and new data won’t be ingested in the Materialized View.\u003c/p\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr class=\"row-even\"\u003e\u003ctd\u003e\u003cp\u003eengine\u003c/p\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003cp\u003eString\u003c/p\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003cp\u003eOptional. Engine for destination Materialized View. Requires the \u003ccode class=\"docutils literal notranslate\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pre\"\u003etype\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e parameter as \u003ccode class=\"docutils literal notranslate\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pre\"\u003ematerialized\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr class=\"row-odd\"\u003e\u003ctd\u003e\u003cp\u003eengine_*\u003c/p\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003cp\u003eString\u003c/p\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003cp\u003eOptional. Engine parameters and options. Requires the \u003ccode class=\"docutils literal notranslate\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pre\"\u003etype\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e parameter as \u003ccode class=\"docutils literal notranslate\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pre\"\u003ematerialized\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e and the \u003ccode class=\"docutils literal notranslate\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pre\"\u003eengine\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e parameter. \u003ca class=\"reference external\" href=\"/docs/api-reference/datasource-api\"\u003eCheck Engine Parameters and Options for more details\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003c/tbody\u003e\n\u003c/table\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eSQL query for the transformation node must be sent in the body encoded in utf-8\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ctable class=\"docutils align-default\" id=\"id10\"\u003e\n\u003ccaption\u003e\u003cspan class=\"caption-text\"\u003eResponse codes\u003c/span\u003e\u003ca class=\"headerlink\" href=\"#id10\" title=\"Permalink to this table\"\u003e¶\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/caption\u003e\n\u003ccolgroup\u003e\n\u003ccol style=\"width: 20.0%\" \u003e\n\u003ccol style=\"width: 80.0%\" \u003e\n\u003c/colgroup\u003e\n\u003cthead\u003e\n\u003ctr class=\"row-odd\"\u003e\u003cth class=\"head\"\u003e\u003cp\u003eCode\u003c/p\u003e\u003c/th\u003e\n\u003cth class=\"head\"\u003e\u003cp\u003eDescription\u003c/p\u003e\u003c/th\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003c/thead\u003e\n\u003ctbody\u003e\n\u003ctr class=\"row-even\"\u003e\u003ctd\u003e\u003cp\u003e200\u003c/p\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003cp\u003eNo error\u003c/p\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr class=\"row-odd\"\u003e\u003ctd\u003e\u003cp\u003e400\u003c/p\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003cp\u003eempty or wrong SQL or API param value\u003c/p\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr class=\"row-even\"\u003e\u003ctd\u003e\u003cp\u003e403\u003c/p\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003cp\u003eForbidden.
